1e:T491af,<h1 id="remarkable-mermaid-plus-plugin-code-analysis" class="group relative text-4xl font-bold mt-8 mb-4 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#remarkable-mermaid-plus-plugin-code-analysis" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Remarkable Mermaid Plus Plugin Code Analysis">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Remarkable Mermaid Plus Plugin Code Analysis
        </h1>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Plugin Version: v1.0.26</strong></p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This article will provide a line-by-line analysis of the <code>remarkable-mermaid-plus</code> plugin code, including the main plugin file <code>index.js</code> and the utility function file <code>mermaid-utils.js</code>. This analysis not only explains the purpose of each line of code but also provides detailed explanations of all non-JavaScript standard library functions and their principles.</p>
<h2 id="overview" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#overview" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Overview">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Overview
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><code>remarkable-mermaid-plus</code> is a plugin for the Remarkable Markdown processor that transforms <code>mermaid</code> code blocks in Markdown into interactive Mermaid diagrams. The plugin works as a post-processor, performing secondary processing on HTML content after Remarkable completes basic rendering.</p>
<h2 id="dependency-library-function-descriptions" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#dependency-library-function-descriptions" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Dependency Library Function Descriptions">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Dependency Library Function Descriptions
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Before diving into the code analysis, let’s understand the main non-standard library functions used by this plugin:</p>
<h3 id="nodejs-related-functions" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#nodejs-related-functions" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Node.js Related Functions">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />

<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>require(moduleName)</code></strong>: Node.js module loading function, used to import external modules or libraries
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Parameters</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>moduleName</code> (string): Module name or path string</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Return Value</strong>: Imported module object or function</li>

<h3 id="remarkable-plugin-api" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#remarkable-plugin-api" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Remarkable Plugin API">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Remarkable Plugin API
        </h3>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>md.render(src, env)</code></strong>: Remarkable’s core rendering method
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Parameters</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>src</code> (string): Input Markdown text string</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>env</code> (Object): Rendering environment object (optional), containing rendering context information</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Return Value</strong>: (string) Rendered HTML string</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Usage Example</strong>:

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="javascript" data-code="%2F%2F%20Render%20basic%20Markdown%20text%0Aconst%20html%20%3D%20md.render('%23%20Hello%20World%5Cn%5CnThis%20is%20**bold**%20text.')%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Render%20with%20environment%20object%0Aconst%20htmlWithEnv%20%3D%20md.render('%23%20Title'%2C%20%7B%20customData%3A%20'value'%20%7D)%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">javascript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment inline">// Render basic Markdown text</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> html = md.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">render</span>(<span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;# Hello World\n\nThis is **bold** text.&#x27;</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment inline">// Render with environment object</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> htmlWithEnv = md.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">render</span>(<span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;# Title&#x27;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr inline">customData</span>: <span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;value&#x27;</span> });
</code></pre>
            </div>
        </li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>originalRender.call(this, src, env)</code></strong>: JavaScript function call method
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Parameters</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>this</code> (Object): Call context (here the Remarkable instance)</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>src</code> (string): Markdown text passed to the original render method</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>env</code> (Object): Environment object passed to the original render method</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Return Value</strong>: (string) Original rendering result</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Usage Example</strong>:

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="javascript" data-code="%2F%2F%20Save%20original%20rendering%20method%0Aconst%20originalRender%20%3D%20md.render%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Override%20rendering%20method%20to%20add%20post-processing%0Amd.render%20%3D%20function(src%2C%20env)%20%7B%0A%2F%2F%20Call%20original%20rendering%20method%0Aconst%20htmlContent%20%3D%20originalRender.call(this%2C%20src%2C%20env)%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Post-process%20HTML%0Areturn%20processHTML(htmlContent)%3B%0A%7D%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">javascript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment inline">// Save original rendering method</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> originalRender = md.<span class="hljs-property inline">render</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment inline">// Override rendering method to add post-processing</span>
md.<span class="hljs-property inline">render</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword inline">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params inline">src, env</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Call original rendering method</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> htmlContent = originalRender.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">call</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_ inline">this</span>, src, env);
  <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Post-process HTML</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword inline">return</span> <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">processHTML</span>(htmlContent);
};
</code></pre>
            </div>
        </li>
</ul></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="browser-dom-api" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#browser-dom-api" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Browser DOM API">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>

        </h3>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>mermaid.initialize(config)</code></strong>: Initialize Mermaid library configuration
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Parameters</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>config</code> (Object): Configuration object, containing the following optional properties:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>theme</code> (string): Theme name, such as 'default’, 'dark’, 'forest’, etc.</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>startOnLoad</code> (boolean): Whether to automatically start rendering on page load</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>securityLevel</code> (string): Security level, 'strict’, 'loose’, ‘sandbox’</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>fontFamily</code> (string): Font family name</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>fontSize</code> (number): Font size</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>flowchart</code> (Object): Flowchart specific configuration</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>sequence</code> (Object): Sequence diagram specific configuration</li>
</ul></li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Return Value</strong>: None</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Usage Example</strong>:

<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>array.some(callback)</code></strong>: Check if at least one element in array satisfies condition
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Parameters</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>callback</code> (function): Test function, receives three parameters:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>element</code> (any): Current element</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>index</code> (number): Current index (optional)</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>array</code> (Array): Original array (optional)</li>
</ul></li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Return Value</strong>: (boolean) Whether there exists an element satisfying the condition</li>

                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">javascript</span>

<h3 id="file-header-and-module-declaration" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">

<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>${mermaidCode}</code>: Embed original Mermaid code</li>
</ul>

</ul>

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Lines 185-187</strong>: Define regular expression to match Mermaid code blocks:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Regular expression explanation</strong>:
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>&lt;pre&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;language-mermaid&quot;&gt;</code>: Match code block start tags</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>([\s\S]*?)</code>: Capture group, match any characters (including newlines)
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>[\s\S]</code>: Match any whitespace or non-whitespace characters (equivalent to matching any character)</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>*?</code>: Non-greedy match, match as few characters as possible</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>&lt;\/code&gt;&lt;\/pre&gt;</code>: Match code block end tags</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>g</code>: Global match flag</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>i</code>: Case-insensitive flag</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

    processMermaidInHTML
};
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Lines 223-225</strong>: Export module:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground"><code>module.exports</code></strong>: Node.js module export mechanism</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">Use object form to export processMermaidInHTML function, convenient for destructuring import</li>
</ul>
<hr class="border-0 h-px bg-gray-300 my-8">
<h2 id="summary" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#summary" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Summary">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Summary
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">The core functionality and features of this plugin include:</p>
<ol class="list-decimal list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Post-processing Architecture</strong>: Doesn’t modify Remarkable’s parsing process, but performs secondary processing after HTML rendering is complete</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Code Block Recognition</strong>: Identifies code blocks in <code>&lt;pre&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;language-mermaid&quot;&gt;</code> format through regular expressions</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Syntax Highlighting Compatibility</strong>: Intelligently processes HTML structures produced by syntax highlighting libraries like highlight.js</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">HTML Entity Decoding</strong>: Correctly processes HTML entities produced during Markdown rendering</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Client-side Rendering</strong>: Generates complete HTML containing Mermaid library and initialization scripts</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Error Handling</strong>: Provides comprehensive error handling and debugging information</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Flexible Configuration</strong>: Supports rich Mermaid configuration options</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">DOM Safety</strong>: Uses temporary containers to avoid DOM operation issues</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="non-standard-library-function-usage-summary" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#non-standard-library-function-usage-summary" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Non-Standard Library Function Usage Summary">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Non-Standard Library Function Usage Summary
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This plugin primarily relies on the following non-JavaScript standard library functions and APIs:</p>
<h4 id="nodejs-ecosystem" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#nodejs-ecosystem" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Node.js Ecosystem">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Node.js Ecosystem
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Module System</strong>: <code>require()</code>, <code>module.exports</code> for module import/export</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">File System</strong>: Relative path module imports</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="remarkable-markdown-processor" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#remarkable-markdown-processor" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Remarkable Markdown Processor">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Remarkable Markdown Processor
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Core Rendering</strong>: <code>md.render()</code> executes Markdown to HTML conversion</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Method Override</strong>: Extends functionality by saving original method references</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="mermaid-chart-library" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#mermaid-chart-library" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Mermaid Chart Library">

            Mermaid Chart Library
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">

<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Initialization</strong>: <code>mermaid.initialize()</code> configures global parameters</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Async Rendering</strong>: <code>mermaid.render()</code> async API renders charts</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="browser-dom-api-1" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#browser-dom-api-1" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Browser DOM API">

                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Browser DOM API
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Element Finding</strong>: <code>document.querySelectorAll()</code> finds target elements</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Element Creation</strong>: <code>document.createElement()</code> creates temporary containers</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">DOM Operations</strong>: <code>appendChild()</code>, <code>removeChild()</code> manages DOM tree</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Content Access</strong>: <code>textContent</code>, <code>innerHTML</code> gets and sets element content</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="regular-expression-processing" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#regular-expression-processing" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Regular Expression Processing">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Regular Expression Processing
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Pattern Matching</strong>: Complex regular expressions match HTML structures</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Content Extraction</strong>: Uses capture groups to extract code block content</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Entity Conversion</strong>: Batch HTML entity decoding</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="async-programming" class="group relative text-xl font-medium mt-4 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#async-programming" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Async Programming">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Async Programming
        </h4>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Timers</strong>: <code>setInterval()</code>, <code>clearInterval()</code> wait for library readiness</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Async Functions</strong>: <code>async/await</code> handles Mermaid async rendering</li>
</ul>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">The plugin achieves seamless integration with Remarkable for Mermaid chart rendering through clever post-processing mechanisms while maintaining good compatibility and error handling capabilities.</p>
